Kasavubu disbanded Congo's parliament after a series of increasingly repressive measures was passed against the political opposition.</span></p></td><td class="cl-958912d4"><p class="cl-95b2e014"><span class="cl-95b2d498">Dominican</span><span class="cl-95b2d498"> </span><span class="cl-95b2d498">Republic</span><span class="cl-95b2d48e"> </span><span class="cl-95b2d48e">initiated</span><span class="cl-95b2d48e"> </span><span class="cl-95b2d498">settle</span><span class="cl-95b2d498"> </span><span class="cl-95b2d498">dispute;sign</span><span class="cl-95b2d498"> </span><span class="cl-95b2d498">formal</span><span class="cl-95b2d498"> </span><span class="cl-95b2d498">agreement</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-95b31acb"><p class="cl-95b2e014"><span class="cl-95b2d48e">215.22</span></p></td><td class="cl-95b31aca"><p class="cl-95b2e014"><span class="cl-95b2d48e">All sides compromised by agreeing on Garcia-Godoy, a moderate, as provisional president.</span></p></td><td class="cl-95b31aca"><p class="cl-95b2e014"><span class="cl-95b2d48e">No</span><span class="cl-95b2d48e"> </span><span class="cl-95b2d48e">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-95b31ac0"><p class="cl-95b2e014"><span class="cl-95b2d48e">215.23</span></p></td><td class="cl-95b31ab6"><p class="cl-95b2e014"><span class="cl-95b2d48e">(Further military incidents occurred in late 1965 and 1966.</span></p></td><td class="cl-95b31ab6"><p class="cl-95b2e014"><span Joaqun Balaguer defeated Juan Bosch and was elected President of the Dominican Republic.)</span></p></td><td class="cl-95b31acc"><p class="cl-95b2e014"><span class="cl-95b2d498">Dominican</span><span troops to the internationally recognized borders, and to repatriate prisoners of war.</span></p></td><td class="cl-95bbf0b4"><p class="cl-95bbc1ca"><span class="cl-95bbb5ea">India;Pakistan</span><span class="cl-95d0aa90"> </span><span class="cl-95d0aa9a">assert</span><span class="cl-95d0aa9a"> </span><span class="cl-95d0aa9a">autonomy</span><span class="cl-95d0aa9a"> </span><span class="cl-95d0aa9a">against</span><span class="cl-95d0aa90"> </span><span class="cl-95d0aa90">toward</span><span class="cl-95d0aa90"> </span><span class="cl-95d0aa9a">United</span><span class="cl-95d0aa9a"> </span><span class="cl-95d0aa9a">Kingdom</span><span class="cl-95d0aa90">.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-95d0e672"><p class="cl-95d0b59e"><span class="cl-95d0aa90">218.10</span></p></td><td class="cl-95d0e669"><p class="cl-95d0b59e"><span class="cl-95d0aa90">Zambia, which itself had become independent on 24 October 1964, viewed the possible establishment of a hostile white-ruled state, independent of the U.K., as a threat to its existence: being landlocked, Zambia was totally dependent on Rhodesia for rail routes to ports, sources of coal and oil, and power from the jointly owned hydroelectric stations at the Kariba Dam on the Rhodesia-Zambia border.</span></p></td><td class="cl-95d0e669"><p class="cl-95d0b59e"><span class="cl-95d0aa9a">Zambia</span><span class="cl-95d0aa90"> </span><span class="cl-95d0aa90">experienced</span><span class="cl-95d0aa90"> </span><span class="cl-95d0aa90">a</span><span class="cl-95d0aa90"> </span><span class="cl-95d0aa9a">fear</span><span class="cl-95d0aa90"> </span><span class="cl-95d0aa90">about</span><span class="cl-95d0aa90"> </span><span class="cl-95d0aa9a">sentence</span><span class="cl-95d0aa9a"> </span><span class="cl-95d0aa9a">9</span><span class="cl-95d0aa90">.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-95d0e65e"><p class="cl-95d0b59e"><span class="cl-95d0aa90">218.11</span></p></td><td class="cl-95d0e668"><p class="cl-95d0b59e"><span class="cl-95d0aa90">The trigger to Zambia's gravest foreign policy crisis was Rhodesia's proclamation of a state of emergency on 5 November 1965, granting the white regime in Salisbury sweeping powers.</span></p></td><td class="cl-95d0e668"><p class="cl-95d0b59e"><span class="cl-95d0aa90">No</span><span class="cl-95d0aa90"> </span><span class="cl-95d0aa90">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-95d0e672"><p class="cl-95d0b59e"><span class="cl-95d0aa90">218.12</span></p></td><td class="cl-95d0e669"><p class="cl-95d0b59e"><span class="cl-95d0aa90">Zambia correctly perceived this to be a prelude to Rhodesia's declaration of independence.</span></p></td><td class="cl-95d0e669"><p class="cl-95d0b59e"><span class="cl-95d0aa9a">Zambia</span><span class="cl-95d0aa90"> </span><span class="cl-95d0aa90">experienced</span><span class="cl-95d0aa90"> </span><span class="cl-95d0aa90">a</span><span </span><span class="cl-95d0aa9a">this</span><span class="cl-95d0aa9a"> </span><span class="cl-95d0aa9a">sentence</span><span class="cl-95d0aa90">.</span><span class="cl-95d0aa90"> </span><span the consequences of such an act.</span></p></td><td class="cl-95d0e668"><p class="cl-95d0b59e"><span class="cl-95d0aa90">No</span><span class="cl-95d0aa90"> </span><span class="cl-95d0e669"><p class="cl-95d0b59e"><span class="cl-95d0aa90">Rhodesian troops were moved to the Zambian border on 9 November.</span></p></td><td class="cl-95d0e669"><p class="cl-95d0b59e"><span class="cl-95d0aa9a">Rhodesia</span><span class="cl-95d0aa90"> </span><span class="cl-95d0aa90">initiated</span><span class="cl-95d0aa90"> </span><span combined the dispatch of troops to the Zambezi River, a promulgation of emergency regulations, and limited economic sanctions against Rhodesia: Rhodesia's currency and money orders would not be class="cl-95d0aa90">218.23</span></p></td><td class="cl-95d0e668"><p class="cl-95d0b59e"><span class="cl-95d0aa90">Zambia, which viewed this suggestion as designed to prevent, rather than prepare for,
